Subject: Educational Codeforces Round 179 (Rated for Div. 2)
Body:
Hello, kasturi_762194.

The series of Educational Rounds continues thanks to the support of the Neapolis University Pafos. They offer a BSc in Computer Science and Artificial Intelligence. The JetBrains Foundation supports this bachelor's program and offers 20 fully funded scholarships for talented first-year students, along with 2 additional scholarships for students wishing to transfer into the second year of the program. Learn more.

You are welcome to register and compete in Educational Codeforces Round 179. he round is partially based on the Saratov Multi-University Olympiad and the Nizhny Novgorod Regional Collegiate Olympiad It starts on Tuesday, June, 3, 2025 14:35 (UTC). The contest duration is 2 hours.

Register Now → The round will be rated for ratings up to 2100.

The goal of educational rounds is to practice and educate, rather than to compete. You can read the details in this post dedicated to them. In short:

* Not only problems, but also exercises can be used.
* Useful ideas will be reused to introduce them to a wider range of participants, even if they are well-known.
* Often the formal text of the statements.
* Rated for Div. 2, unrated for Div. 1.
* ICPC rules + 12-hour open hacking phase.

The allowed programming languages are C/C++, Pascal, Java, C#, Python, Ruby, Perl, PHP, Haskell, Scala, OCaml, Go, D, JavaScript, Rust and Kotlin.

The round will be held on the rules of Educational Rounds, so read the rules (here) beforehand. The round will be for newcomers and participants from both divisions. But the difficulty of problems is for Div 2. Want to compete? Do not forget to register for the contest and check your handle on the registrants page. The registration will be open for the whole contest duration.

If you have any questions, please feel free to ask me on the pages of Codeforces. If you no longer wish to receive these emails, click https://codeforces.com/unsubscribe/contests/67ce226b8a2a9e954b093486a3157cc5d8359653/ to unsubscribe.

Wish you high rating, MikeMirzayanov and Codeforces team

REGISTER   Participants will solve five progressively complex tasks focused on building efficient voting systems. Each task is crafted to test different aspects of smart contract development:

From: noreply@codeforces.com
Subject: Kotlin Heroes: Episode 12 [100 t-shirts, money prizes!]
Body:


Attention! The round starts on Monday, April, 7, 2025 14:35 (UTC).  Hello, kasturi_762194.

We are happy to announce the twelfth "Kotlin Heroes" competition which will be held on Codeforces! Kotlin Heroes: Episode 12 is open for everybody, regardless of a division. We will be glad to see you among the participants!

It starts on Monday, April, 7, 2025 14:35 (UTC). The contest duration is 2.5 hours. You are allowed to use Kotlin only to solve the problems.

Register Now →  The round writers are BledDest, awoo, adedalic and Neon. Don't miss the round!

Top three winners will get prizes of $512, $256, and $128 respectively, top 50 will win a Kotlin Heroes t-shirt and exclusive Kotlin stickers, competitors solving at least one problem will enter into a draw for one of 50 Kotlin Heroes t-shirts.

Please note that we are not able to ship prizes to any country, state, province, or territory subject to comprehensive OFAC sanctions, including Belarus, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Russia, Syria, or the Crimea, Donetsk, or Luhansk regions. For complete the list, please visit this page.

The round is held in accordance with slightly modified ICPC rules:

* The round is unrated.
* The contest will have 6-10 problems of various levels of complexity.
* You are allowed to only use Kotlin to solve these problems.
* Participants are ranked according to the number of correctly solved problems.
* Ties are resolved based on the lowest total penalty time for all problems, which is computed as follows. For each solved problem, a penalty is set to the submission time of that problem (the time since the start of the contest). An extra penalty of 10 minutes is added for each failed submission on solved problems (i.e., if you never solve the problem, you will not be penalized for trying that problem). If two participants solved the same number of problems and scored the same penalty, then those of them who had previously made the last successful submission will be given an advantage in the distribution of prizes and gifts.

Want to compete? Do not forget to register for the contest and check your handle on the registrants page.

To help you get familiar with Kotlin JetBrains has prepared a tutorial on competitive programming in Kotlin and a practice round, where you can try to solve a few simple problems in Kotlin. All solutions are open, which means that you can look at a solution even if you haven't solved a problem yet. The practice round is available by the link.

If you have any questions, please feel free to ask me on the pages of Codeforces. If you no longer wish to receive these emails, click https://codeforces.com/unsubscribe/contests/67ce226b8a2a9e954b093486a3157cc5d8359653/ to unsubscribe.

The series of Educational Rounds continues thanks to the support of the Neapolis University Pafos. They offer a BSc in Computer Science and Artificial Intelligence. The JetBrains Foundation supports this bachelor's program and offers 20 fully funded scholarships for the most talented applicants. Learn more.

You are welcome to register and compete in Educational Codeforces Round 177. The round is based on the problems from the Open Championship of Karelia in competitive programming. It starts on Thursday, April, 3, 2025 14:35 (UTC). The contest duration is 2 hours.

Register Now → The round will be rated for ratings up to 2100.

The goal of educational rounds is to practice and educate, rather than to compete. You can read the details in this post dedicated to them. In short:

* Not only problems, but also exercises can be used.
* Useful ideas will be reused to introduce them to a wider range of participants, even if they are well-known.
* Often the formal text of the statements.
* Rated for Div. 2, unrated for Div. 1.
* ICPC rules + 12-hour open hacking phase.

The allowed programming languages are C/C++, Pascal, Java, C#, Python, Ruby, Perl, PHP, Haskell, Scala, OCaml, Go, D, JavaScript, Rust and Kotlin.

The round will be held on the rules of Educational Rounds, so read the rules (here) beforehand. The round will be for newcomers and participants from both divisions. From: "MongoDB" <mongodb@team.mongodb.com>
Subject: Upcoming changes to Atlas
Body:
<https://www.mongodb.com/>

Introducing the New Navigation Experience for MongoDB Atlas 






Hi Kastu,



MongoDB is refreshing the Atlas navigation to deliver a more efficient, 
seamless, and productive experience to our customers. These changes will begin 
rolling out the week of April 7th, 2025.




Here's a quick overview of what's changing: 

 * Simplified Project Navigation: The side navigation has been redesigned for 
rapid access to key tools, enabling faster navigation of the Atlas platform 
through four sections: Database, Data, Services, and Security.
 * Clearer Resource Context: The updated top navigation bar, the resource 
navigator, ensures developers always know which resource (e.g., project, 
organization, cluster) they are working on. Switching between resources is now 
simpler, with improved context clarity as users navigate deeper into Atlas. The 
workflow now negates any need to backtrack to a project’s overview.
 * Centralized Utilities Hub: Essential utilities like Alerts, Help, Billing, 
and Identity and Access Management (IAM) are consolidated in one location at 
the top-right corner. This ensures rapid access and saves time. Users can also 
access the product menu to findMongoDB University <https://learn.mongodb.com/>, 
Documentation <https://www.mongodb.com/docs/>, Dev Center 
<https://www.mongodb.com/developer/>, Community Forums 
<https://www.mongodb.com/community/forums/>, and Support 
<https://support.mongodb.com/>. 
 * Atlas Charts Relocation: Atlas Charts will now be accessible via the 
Visualization heading in theData section of the left-side navigation panel.


Below is a sneak peek at what the primary side navigation for Atlas will look 
like on a project level.



Note: MongoDB will roll out the new navigation experience to Atlas 
organizations in phases to ensure a smooth transition to the new navigation.



The new navigation will start rolling out on April 7th, 2025. It will take 
approximately6 to 8 weeks for the navigation to become available to all Atlas 
organizations. All users will experience the new navigation by June 2025.



If you have further questions, please contact your Account Executive or our 
Support Team <https://support.mongodb.com/>.



Best,
MongoDB Atlas Team

Body:
Here are a few resources to help you get started. 







Welcome to MongoDB 




Ready to get your first MongoDB cluster up and running? Start with these four 
steps:

 * Create cluster 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/tutorial/deploy-free-tier-cluster/>
 * Add IP address to access list 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/security/add-ip-address-to-list/>
 * Create a user 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/tutorial/create-mongodb-user-for-cluster/>
 * Connect to cluster 
<https://www.mongodb.com/docs/atlas/tutorial/connect-to-your-cluster/>



 

If you’re more of a visual learner, we’ve put together a six-minute video 
<https://learn.mongodb.com/courses/getting-started-with-mongodb-atlas> that 
guides you through cluster setup.

 <https://learn.mongodb.com/courses/getting-started-with-mongodb-atlas>

Next, you can start building. Populate your newly-created cluster with some of 
our sample datasets. These are great for testing and quick prototyping.



Get started 
<https://account.mongodb.com/account/login?n=https%3A%2F%2Fcloud.mongodb.com%2Fgo%3Fl%3Dhttps%3A%2F%2Fcloud.mongodb.com%2Fv2%2F%3Cproject%3E%26h%3Dclusters%2Fdetail%2F%3Ccluster%3E>

From: Codeforces@codeforces.com
Subject: Educational Codeforces Round 176 (Rated for Div. 2)
Body:
Hello, kasturi_762194.

The series of Educational Rounds continues thanks to the support of the Neapolis University Pafos. They offer a BSc in Computer Science and Artificial Intelligence. The JetBrains Foundation supports this bachelor's program and offers 15 fully funded scholarships for the most talented applicants. Learn more.

You are welcome to register and compete in Educational Codeforces Round 176. It starts on Monday, March, 17, 2025 14:35 (UTC). The contest duration is 2 hours.

Register Now → The round will be rated for ratings up to 2100.

The goal of educational rounds is to practice and educate, rather than to compete. You can read the details in this post dedicated to them. In short:

* Not only problems, but also exercises can be used.
* Useful ideas will be reused to introduce them to a wider range of participants, even if they are well-known.
* Often the formal text of the statements.
* Rated for Div. 2, unrated for Div. 1.
* ICPC rules + 12-hour open hacking phase.

The allowed programming languages are C/C++, Pascal, Java, C#, Python, Ruby, Perl, PHP, Haskell, Scala, OCaml, Go, D, JavaScript, Rust and Kotlin.

The round will be held on the rules of Educational Rounds, so read the rules (here) beforehand. The round will be for newcomers and participants from both divisions. But the difficulty of problems is for Div 2. Want to compete? Do not forget to register for the contest and check your handle on the registrants page. The registration will be open for the whole contest duration.

If you have any questions, please feel free to ask me on the pages of Codeforces. If you no longer wish to receive these emails, click https://codeforces.com/unsubscribe/contests/67ce226b8a2a9e954b093486a3157cc5d8359653/ to unsubscribe.

Wish you high rating, MikeMirzayanov and Codeforces team

From: Codeforces@codeforces.com
Subject: Educational Codeforces Round 175 (Rated for Div. 2)
Body:
Hello, kasturi_762194.

The series of Educational Rounds continues thanks to the support of the Neapolis University Pafos. They offer a BSc in Computer Science and AI with JetBrains Scholarships. Gain cutting-edge skills in AI and machine learning, preparing you for high-demand tech careers.

You are welcome to register and compete in Educational Codeforces Round 175. It starts on Thursday, February, 27, 2025 14:35 (UTC). The contest duration is 2 hours.

Register Now → The round will be rated for ratings up to 2100.

The goal of educational rounds is to practice and educate, rather than to compete. You can read the details in this post dedicated to them. In short:

* Not only problems, but also exercises can be used.
* Useful ideas will be reused to introduce them to a wider range of participants, even if they are well-known.
* Often the formal text of the statements.
* Rated for Div. 2, unrated for Div. 1.
* ICPC rules + 12-hour open hacking phase.

The allowed programming languages are C/C++, Pascal, Java, C#, Python, Ruby, Perl, PHP, Haskell, Scala, OCaml, Go, D, JavaScript, Rust and Kotlin.

The round will be held on the rules of Educational Rounds, so read the rules (here) beforehand. The round will be for newcomers and participants from both divisions. But the difficulty of problems is for Div 2. Want to compete? Do not forget to register for the contest and check your handle on the registrants page. The registration will be open for the whole contest duration.

If you have any questions, please feel free to ask me on the pages of Codeforces. If you no longer wish to receive these emails, click https://codeforces.com/unsubscribe/contests/67ce226b8a2a9e954b093486a3157cc5d8359653/ to unsubscribe.

Wish you high rating, MikeMirzayanov and Codeforces team

From: Google Play <googleplay-noreply@google.com>
Subject: 
 Upcoming changes to your settings
Body:


Hi Kastu,


We're piloting changes to Google Play purchase verification to give you new  
controls over your purchase experience.


Play purchase verification helps prevent unauthorized purchases on your  
device. Currently, you can choose to require Play purchase verification  
always, every 30 minutes, or never. However, some payment methods include  
their own, separate verification process. For those payment methods, you  
currently have to complete verification twice if you also have Play  
verification turned on.


Soon, this setting will change so that you can choose whether to require  
Play verification for payment methods that already include a separate  
verification process. In particular, this change will affect payments made  
through UPI and netbanking, because they have their own verification  
processes (e.g. PIN based verification on UPI).


*Important:* This update may affect settings you have previously chosen. To  
check your current settings in the Google Play app, tap the profile icon at  
the top right > Settings > Purchase verification.


This update will impact your current setting choice as described below. You  
can always choose to change your settings, including requiring Play  
verification for all purchases, once these updates are available.

...


Current setting selection


If you've chosen to require Play verification “Always” or “Every 30  
minutes” and you're above 18


*Example 1:* If you pay with UPI, you need to complete Play verification,  
through biometrics or your Google Account password, then UPI PIN  
verification.


*Example 2:* If you pay with a gift card, you need to complete Play  
verification through biometrics or your Google Account password.


New setting selection (coming soon)


You'll no longer complete Play verification for payment methods that  
include a separate verification process, specifically UPI and netbanking.


*Example 1:* If you pay with UPI, you'll only need to complete UPI PIN  
verification.


*Example 2:* If you pay with a gift card, you'll continue to complete Play  
verification.


Current setting selection


If you've chosen to require Play verification “Always” or “Every 30  
minutes” and you're under 18


New setting selection (coming soon)


You'll continue to be required to complete Play verification for all  
purchases.


Current setting selection


If you've chosen to require Play verification “Never”


New setting selection (coming soon)


You'll continue to make purchases without Play verification.

...

We'll notify you soon when these changes take effect.


See your Google Play Order History  
<"https://play.google.com/store/account/orderhistory">.

View the Google Play Refund Policy  
<"https://support.google.com/googleplay/answer/2479637#apps"}> and the  
Terms of Service  
<"https://play.google.com/intl/en-US/about/play-terms.html"}>.

Welcome to Gemini, your upgraded AI assistant from Google that can help you  
supercharge your creativity and productivity. Gemini can not only provide  
the hands-free help that you love from Google Assistant, but can go far  
beyond in conversationality and richness of the tasks it can help with.  
With Gemini on your phone, you can now have a natural, free-flowing voice  
conversation through Gemini Live1, and get help writing, creating,  
learning, and more. Gemini will now serve as your Android device’s primary  
assistant. Learn  
more<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5rx62qgnW2jCCTx-KKdj4cxotJF-2KOxH9HREtTEU_ClaODWIh7fTfIsaT2eBHJMXy6NL4bZ_4u12uejq4iQ55vCEDKjzUUTdnJUd-mypPdfaXfSZuMbY3WdWv91dotnDwJm3ebp2Z1s9QrZ33GWgiR8LA6gU0vsmo-Kk1zQVOnJGLzVrijZZubARu67cft-QrJQzAPT6dkbfw9JCexfmY74N3zNy5WSQWx2VLxvEwTfX9Dxd1Ri5j3>  
about what you can do with Gemini.

If you wish to switch your device’s primary assistant to Google Assistant,  
you can do that in Settings. How to  
switch<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5rogi12G8qUXFx2Yj9GP5RxwFl4kWEfxJhjg4ZeyU1u44HJu9ryTBJWwSGrbZ9Ta7Oi8gmsgLEbQ8y9G-jsJ-HvrcnzfGVL01yd30K7XX529N_5_jcgjDJx2J3SesY8UX2tyquFGqURbSEdrYQJSg6_ppPfWn_jv9dvSk7zItfVflCzZXbX7g>.

How Gemini handles data and works with other services

Gemini uses info from your devices and services to help you

Gemini uses info from your devices and services to provide more customized  
and context-aware assistance. Gemini accesses certain system permissions  
and data (including through Google Assistant), like call and message logs,  
contacts (to help you keep in touch), and screen content (to help you act  
on it).

Gemini works with Google Assistant

Gemini gets help from Google Assistant for certain actions. When that  
happens, relevant Assistant settings such as Personal Results apply. When  
Gemini handles actions through Extensions, those Google Assistant settings  
won’t apply. Learn  
more<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5pC7G47G7uqz2DMJ9SFlvxvICssgjhGl8FQesP2qkKziUOtlNQodHEAvKrOPZZ9oF-UwMiLMaZfMJsL5JGGkq1cebrwzTB3bwokNzRRYgme9VRR6ONEm8C8gSr-VD2jU8uzfRd41XFTfUaxHnkQ3_bBioENbBVGk5Zmc8RGzCcRlR_efkqxPjnmeu7-FSlv3WoXt11_xadr33wuu7qhrlkMt_UVfQWOtLoQ23jqifPkr4AEurfmijA>.

Gemini Extensions

With Extensions, Gemini can respond with real-time info from other  
services, like Google Maps and YouTube. You can also choose to connect  
services like Google Workspace and YouTube Music. If Gemini finds an  
Extension that can help, it will send information from your conversation,  
and other relevant information, to that Extension to help it generate a  
better response. You can manage your Gemini Extensions settings. Learn  
more<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5qSIz-VRqZbl1bg4rkCHhrbAi6zKdbgN34n281zkwHbZrbYDDsoLlvW0pFhmA_DvGQq14l6F2ucPBWmeSf8s7cUw-feN1T_tigcTrac_nXo_QCOTTXcnHjKNSPDTB3E-zAEHOdzmgrJpDNMgGtan6vWSU6fAluaIZPd_w1dvww9F9WfeeTSdnkGwDQYQr080EsMYYGuvD6zclyNFBHiZwZ3CJk3-veZ0hWxoA6zBwEvIW0f6QnorTpdsVaWZg>.

Things to know when speaking to Gemini

If “Hey Google” & Voice  
Match<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5pcznoUv_-Z1tZAcn8sOYvg75XHGctCpK4mnos2LKI84Ksxt0xBSMBn652WZNFr0p_Dp1CFQIH4JVQsOh_asWe4ae0Q4GILlcF2EyyU_Ur7VNZztpoDg5pYSXPg7s8zBnQRyuv3IpaJGGJ1vFIxL0HnLEavURIkFBaeGD-nUr3TEG2EoMq6BK7YhIwyaXfbISNHZvNSl5ziNNAuOurFD0PuNbywuDV50-9XOPsyoxqxfoJPW6Vsf-I98U-kr2hWEG2kxxRGPPfNPIR4Jmps6vLTEef0IDUmaXzqObk8Qb9sfUqCiOuz6RrBYiKykI_1G6gDUqwjBfVyxYQlb3IYGHODoilok-dxtESvtIt3YK9WKnQlVm0j5qWCTOtonZeEpDtfhQJ-YHvmOISgOlcgGAAGR1w1yMVh>  
(powered by Google Assistant) are on in Settings, you can talk to your  
assistant hands-free. Gemini may activate when you didn’t intend it to, for  
example, if it detects a noise like “Hey Google,” or if you accidentally  
activate it by touch. If Gemini responds, it will treat your input like a  
normal activation.

Gemini responses on lock screen

Gemini helps you with answers and actions even when your device is locked.  
To protect your privacy, Gemini will still require you to unlock for some  
actions, for example when responses contain your personal content from apps  
(such as calendar events). You can change your Gemini on lock screen  
settings. Learn  
more<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5q6gFxA-GTiO5Ats6SxIyP-wj33k9i6y-qGMi23JAjgNYp9fngFHMWZtT54WQDG2flBztiA3YVcTtcHwIEXwR4blrjcDqM817xBwUl5GJ1jpMtA66CIlqjVQ2EeeqH95jy6yJzA4ZsGeeBecTcFo66ZHQJLCExL9b1Y18Oq-NvY>.

Gemini activity and your choices

When you use Gemini, Google collects your activity, like your chats and  
location info. This data is stored in your Google Account and used to  
improve Google AI and services with help from trained reviewers. You can  
manage your Gemini Apps Activity  
settings<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5qBu9_td2Ge1BmqX0MuYDnHqwMQEblJDVzlN8TUta20T0KPWdzAuQ085bi2qE0oHpOBvkFmzAfS0jrNkKMNOC1fb52pjWcxczZiB2LNJ16fFpH3qyfm8pljDi--Z3aaOyNwZL9URORFj2qmlkyvohyxzv0fzkHyYVwtRE2uJNRNDDm5Nz2E_dZj4F1BK8E7m1Axx3yuf8gjaXiyWnnnGBEiC1Sd>.  
Don’t enter info you wouldn’t want reviewed or used. Learn  
more<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5oE3OIwV2e6fNXFlPbyr2-49acI4NqzwmaC7LmhVpFDX1eBIAQoHIJZQ4mbc3imdxANEOwlz7Iy9ffl6Sgo2-tBWLJj_caBolXX2s6nk0PMldG4oiahsyXk54IFubAi1JvTQGgrx6un6m2rdg1bwDpwgoSFX79Xu4Rgq7bGFXS9kLKIT246OfK68BQYnCv9biD8gYj9B-e7sXnaYsvipVnXnmvA22ufHnByOiChs71ubyBYCEYi-p02-KfbIeHTEaD2qVVf2kPYvcPljQzjRlb9faExNv6t76t301ciCjbUlMWNgxzSCKtQ5f_5nlUGZw4HHngEjYk4BAUXmd0SIg2Dx9_pOrJS-d8mk_Tk_dPZo7YE-5gT72rYzjryq8FU4f0jmwX5Llzig1Q5hkZrPbAT3M7VM12tEx3Fl49DykyLA2nAAV3BPh0KRBO3ZT3WUaGziPcmbSWk_Rgp3pQK0l4TmtirS6_baUwiOONjc7-kH7A9lKjjRpdv2G14T7gXmD9fTaVh4Q>.

From: Sarah from pdfFiller <sarah@pdffiller.com>
Subject: Organize your documents for easy navigation
Body:
Discover how to organize your documents into personal and shared folders with pdfFiller.

‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

Organize documents in folders →

Easily search and navigate documents stored in your account

Keep your documents organized and secure in pdfFiller’s cloud storage using various types of folders.

Organize documents in folders:
https://link.pdffiller.com/r?u=290753153&m=4273799468&t=34177&o=AIdbiAgqVAlub297_MqgVMOMtXkn3vY95LfRUD_leTSgJTDRutjwFAlo5IsNzL05pU8gWarr7G-wDBfCqqJvHVLaSQAk02LDMMlkW9I5C-I4FLbO26UEFl-WejEUP-EGYImZYN8fFxy3BDWkWbmwrXNuJWU_xwZkCz804TQKlTVC6rRWP6Rwi_sXQmWxSSJ38AglZCuBx8wpRZ2bHHUeFwXMxwsYUkiX2-PXsbP7FFZffYXWRg%3D%3D&s=direct_push

Personal folders: Manage your documents without giving access to anyone else

Shared folders: Share documents and templates with your team members

Encrypted folder: Securely store your sensitive documents in a password‍-‍protected folder

Smart folders: Automatically sort documents based on their tags

How to manage your folders

To view your custom folders, go to My Docs > Documents in the header menu. You can conveniently sort files by Type, People, Activity, and Tags.

Create a new folder by clicking Add new > Create folder in the left-hand menu. Enter the name of your new folder, decide who can access it (make the folder personal or shared), and click Create.

To create a subfolder, click “...” next to a parent folder and select Create subfolder.

Move documents to specific folders by clicking “...” next to a file and selecting More > Move to Folder. Or simply drag and drop a file in the desired folder.

To enable shared access, click “...” next to a folder and select Share folder. Then, specify the contacts with whom you will share access and give necessary permissions.

Create organization →

Create your shared team space with Organizations

Invite your entire team to edit, eSign, and share documents quickly and securely.

Create organization:
https://link.pdffiller.com/r?u=290753153&m=4270463217&t=34176&o=lmPWEunz_8GETPbWXwFY2116jmQMiVe3TXA1niOAMN8qu5P4UDOwbXSHTKfmunqBJFh1Y89iL-jnMuZl2LLddy8X7vucg12kTPIuqon6SyJcxW8BWihHgpUr0LDXdyFe4tPDgqWcNXTqjdeG3mM7eAVYGD-t3VxfrNDc8R_hLFp0Lut4xYmWlSaPZzFeLJFsC1T-GypCmwnpxUth8OjXEbEzePikSMInYXeuyTE%3D&s=direct_push

Why create an Organization in pdfFiller?

Collaboration: Equip your team with every necessary tool to edit, eSign, manage, and share PDF documents from anywhere.

Shared access: Allow your teammates to access shared folders, documents, and templates.

Security: Ensure secure log‍-‍in for your entire team with SSO and two‍-‍step verification.

Insights: Track user activity and download reports to evaluate your team’s performance and acknowledge top contributors.

How to create an Organization

Go to your account settings and select the Organizations tab. Then, click Create Organization and enter your organization’s name. Job’s done!

Click Invite to add users. You can invite users by email or by sharing an invite link.

Set access levels for users: Members can only view and edit their documents while Admins can also track user activity and manage other users in your organization.

From: Sarah from pdfFiller <sarah@pdffiller.com>
Subject: Document management + CRM? pdfFiller is the best of both worlds
Body:
Learn how to manage your contacts and shared documents in pdfFiller.

‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌ ‌

Add contacts →

Access all your contacts and shared documents in one place

Similar to popular CRMs, pdfFiller allows you to save your contacts and their details, track related documents and activities, and easily send documents for review, editing, or eSignature.

Add contacts:
https://link.pdffiller.com/r?u=290753153&m=4254527470&t=34175&o=ORvAxgeHoqfjtD2_K-XfLl_PMzQehz7cLlG8jmni7aPnfXr2915ttqT4p2C0aAtJGCpT6VBvR40ZQ9oZ6cDJciGrR3lPVIM3VNErrxGK_JBaPOGOkdY3dbxhIQ-3r6baKxCQq8xUuJEqzEGgwDDtCh4EgqmbCPW6tK4vG6l-WFF1fcMdDbOp94aSQ1Caw26K1-y7_A%3D%3D&s=direct_push

How does this feature make your life easier?

Get a CRM-like experience at no extra cost

Manage all your contacts and their information from a single location in your account

Share and send documents for eSignature faster by quickly adding recipients from your saved contacts

Track your interactions with every client, team member, or vendor﻿ ﻿–﻿ ﻿view shared documents, activities, attachments, notes, and audit trails

How to manage contacts in pdfFiller

Go to Contacts in the pdfFiller dashboard.

Select any contact to view its information, related documents, and activities.

You can edit your contacts or send documents to specific recipients directly from the Contacts menu.

pdfFiller saves the contacts you interact with automatically, but you can also add them manually by clicking Add new > Add contact.

pdfFiller also allows you to quickly import multiple contacts from your Google account.

The goal of educational rounds is to practice and educate, rather than to compete. You can read the details in this post dedicated to them. In short:

* Not only problems, but also exercises can be used.
* Useful ideas will be reused to introduce them to a wider range of participants, even if they are well-known.
* Often the formal text of the statements.
* Rated for Div. 2, unrated for Div. 1.
* ICPC rules + 12-hour open hacking phase.

The round will be held on the rules of Educational Rounds, so read the rules (here) beforehand. The round will be for newcomers and participants from both divisions. Quick sharing via a document link delivered right to your recipient’s inbox

Easy access management to prevent unwanted changes in your documents

How to share a document with pdfFiller

Select a document and click Share in the right‍-‍hand toolbar.

Enter the recipient’s email address or add your saved contacts.

Set permissions: allow the recipient to review or edit your document.

Click Share to send an email with an invitation to review or edit your document.

You can also copy a link to your document and share it with anyone.

What can you do with templates?

Save time by instantly generating copies of essential documents

How to create a reusable template

Add fillable fields to your document or pre-fill it with necessary data.

Save your document and click Convert to template.

To generate a fresh document copy, select the template you need and click Create from template.

Customize a newly created document before sharing by completing fillable fields or making necessary edits.

How does pdfFiller simplify eSigning?

Prepare, send, and track documents within a single workspace

No need to switch between different apps and accounts

How to eSign a document

Select the Sign tool and create your electronic signature by typing, drawing, or using other methods.

Place your eSignature anywhere in a document and adjust its size.

How to send a document for eSignature

Click Edit Fillable Fields in the right‍-‍hand sidebar and select Recipients in the header menu.

Add signers by entering their email addresses.

Insert one or multiple signature fields in your document and select a signer role for each field.

Click Review and send to finalize your eSignature request. Set a signing order, schedule notifications, and send your document.

platform, including videos, comments, links and thumbnails. In addition to  
Community Guidelines, creators who want to monetise content on YouTube must  
comply with  
<https://notifications.google.com/g/p/ANiao5rEz_1w7FvpYNFxnuXph4aEjLbvGtWTwpyM6F4l0_bQGlCS1SNhnlnRMmCx0zs51v3gk6-I39qMuCKmvib5d8NjyFZ--I2892_w0SnZixPWwj1mt0nenxesWN-Nj3Jo0Ida0G8nxEgDvEs5OjT0mzpwagfEnAuf6t-lnONl4OrOmwJPNKvqWpU0qOs4pEb8noDjg3mCB9CltDQMah5cTL2ed_VpLqLzW-Q8MbgPf4Qy3JkHvpdbhEm8aws4d84Yg7wuscCok5tKrucpXSMYyGV7C9K2wzp8RsxyuzCV_o-h_VvFtcBX0zZY">Monetization  
Policies.




By way of due diligence as an intermediary we also take this opportunity to  
remind our users to comply with the Indian Information Technology  
(Intermediary Guidelines and Digital Media Ethics Code) Rules, 2021 (as  
amended) (“Intermediary Rules”).



YouTube is also again informing you under Rule 5 of the Intermediary Rules  
that if you are a publisher of news or current affairs content, you are  
required to furnish the details of your accounts on YouTube to the Ministry  
of Information and Broadcasting (“MIB”) in compliance with Rules 18 of the  
Intermediary Rules and public notice dated 26 May 2021 published by MIB.



Please adhere to these terms to maintain continued use of and access to  
YouTube. Violation of these terms and guidelines may result in warnings or  
further action including loss of access or termination of all or part of  
your account.
